Et quant il est desaluez dou tot, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et le tigne I ministres fors par la jambe, desus la cheville; puis trai le piet a toi a ta main destre, et puis a la senestre II fois, puis l’estent en haut, et boute bellement lou piet en haut; et fai ce II fois, si com nos avons dit, em boutant et en traiant lou piet; s’elle revient, c’est bien; se ce non, si rencomence l’ovraige, car il revient; et s’il ne puet revenir ensi, si fai gesir lou malaide sor son dos sus terre, et fiche I passeil fermement en terre entre ses cuixes, et lie drapelz entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide; puis teigne li ministres la cuixe, et uns autres ministres estende lou piet a ses mains ou a I liien, k’il lie sus le col dou piet; puis estende chescuns ministres igalment, et li passelz soit adés entre les cuixes dou malaide por retenir le malaide quant on l’estent; puis mette li mires igal la dislocation a ses mains, et uns autres ministres teigne la jambe sainne au desoz, et li dislocation revenra hastanment.	 And when it is completely dislocated, you must make the patient sit straight, and hold him by the leg above the ankle; then pull the foot to yourself with your right hand, and then with the left hand twice, then lift it up, and push the foot forcefully upwards; and do this twice, as we have said, pushing and pulling the foot; if it returns, that's good; if not, start again, for it may return; and if it cannot return, lay the patient on his back on the ground, and insert a splint firmly into the ground between his knees, and tie rags around it so as not to hurt the patient; then hold the leg of the minister, and another minister holds the sound leg above the knee or ankle, keeping him raised on the neck of the foot; then each minister holds evenly, and the splint should be close between the patient's knees to hold the patient when lifting; then place the mirrors equally around the dislocation with their hands, and another minister holds the sound leg below, and the dislocation will quickly return.
Et quant elle iert a point, si met l’emplastre et estoupes sus, et l’estrain forment, et lie lou piet a la jambe, et warde les ners qui sont sus la cheville derrier, que li liiens ne soit trop estrois; puis le laisse II jors ou III, et se li liiens amolist, si l’estrain; puis le deslie au tier jor ou au quart, et deffent a aler lou malaide par IIII jors; et s’il va devant cel termine, ce n’est mie seurtez qu’il ne desalue encor.	 And when it is in place, put the plaster and stopper on top, press down firmly, tie the foot to the leg, and watch the nerves that are above the ankle to make sure they are not too tight; then leave it for two or three days, and if the ligament softens, tighten it; then untie it on the third or fourth day, and let the patient walk for four days; and if he goes before the deadline, it is not certain that he will not dislocate again.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si covient que tu l’apaises, si com nos avons dit autre part, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if an abscess swells up, you must calm it as we have said elsewhere, until it is healthy.
des dois	of the two [shoulders]
Quant li doi sont desaluez, si les covient bellement estendre sens travail, et c’est legiere chose.	When both shoulders are dislocated, they must be carefully stretched out without strain, and it is an easy thing to do.
Et se li dislocations est en aucun nout dou dos dou piet, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide sus I leu plain ou sus .ie. table tot droit, et met ton piet sus ce qui apert de ces jointures, puis presse a ton piet forment, tant qu’il reviegne; et quant il est igalz, et il n’i apert nient, si met desoz la plante dou piet une table a II chiés, puis l’estrain forment, et le laisse III jors, puis le deslie; et le fai reposer, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 If the dislocation is in any way towards the back of the foot, you must make the patient sit on a flat surface or table straight up, place your foot over the opening of the joints, then press down firmly until it goes back; when it is even and there is no longer an opening, put two fingers under the foot's heel, then tighten it for three days, then untie it; and let him rest until he recovers.
de plaie et de dislocation ensamble	Of wounds and dislocations together
Quant plaie vient avec la dislocation, et on la vuet restorer, maintes fois avient que li malaides muert: si ne soies mie presumptuous en la cure, se tu n’es saiges en l’art et tu ne l’as useit longement, et se tu n’es pitous et misericors et tardis, ne mie hardis; et use au comencement de choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et laisse le malaide en la main Deu, se tu n’i vois esperance de santeit; et quant tu i vois esperance, si ramoinne maintenant le membre au leu, ainsois que li apostemes chaus i viegne; et quant li membres est a leu, si aministre choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et cure la plaie, si com il covient, d’oignemens desiccatis; et se avec la dislocation a brisure, et os menus desevrez, si les oste, et fai ce que nos avons dit en maladies simples; et te garde d’entrer en voie de paour, selonc ce que j’ai dit, car ce te vaut mues selonc ton Creator, et por la saveteit de t’arme et de ton cors.	 When a wound comes with dislocation and it is to be restored, many times the patient dies: do not be presumptuous in the cure, unless you are wise in the art and have used it for a long time, and unless you are compassionate, merciful, and slow, yet cautious; and first use cooling remedies against abscesses, and leave the patient in God's hands if you see no hope of health; and when you see hope, reset the limb to its place as soon as the abscess heals; and when the limb is in place, administer cooling remedies against abscesses, and treat the wound, as necessary, with strong drying agents; and if with dislocation there is fracture, and small bones are displaced, set them, and do as we have said for simple diseases; and beware of entering into fear, according to what I've said, for it will harm you according to your Creator, and for the sake of the wisdom of your weapon and body.
Amen	 Amen (Literally: So be it)
